library( "DBI")
library( "RMySQL")
library( "GDD")
dbd <- dbDriver( "MySQL")

base <- dbGetQuery( con, "(select subplot.id as subplot_id, rcode, scode, pcode, ptype, subplot.number as sp_number, subplot.treatment from subplot, (select plot.id as plot_id, rcode, scode, plot.code as pcode, plot.type as ptype from plot, (select site.id as site_id, rcode, site.code as scode from site, (select region.id as region_id, region.code as rcode from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region_id) as r where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=r.region_id order by site_id) as s where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=s.site_id order by plot_id) as p where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=p.plot_id order by subplot_id) ")
subplot <- list()
set <- list()
attr <- list()
out <- data.frame()

vf_v595 <- dbGetQuery( con, "select subplot.id as subplot_id, subplot.sage_condition_pse as sp_phase from subplot, (select plot.id from plot, (select site.id from site, (select region.id from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region.id) as regions  where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=regions.id order by site.id) as sites  where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=sites.id order by plot.id) as plots  where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=plots.id order by subplot.id")

attr <- c( attr, list( vf_v595))
rm( vf_v595)


vf_v596 <- dbGetQuery( con, "select subplot.id as subplot_id, plots.elevation_m as p_elevation from subplot, (select plot.id, plot.elevation_m from plot, (select site.id from site, (select region.id from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region.id) as regions  where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=regions.id order by site.id) as sites  where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=sites.id order by plot.id) as plots  where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=plots.id order by subplot_id")

attr <- c( attr, list( vf_v596))
rm( vf_v596)


res <- dbSendQuery( con, "select subplot_id, year, speriod, concat( substring( veg_volume.subplot_sample_id, 1, 2), '.', substring( veg_volume.subplot_sample_id, 4, 2), '.', species_txn) as id, diameter_longest_cm as dia1, diameter_perp_cm as dia2, height_cm as hgt, ((pi()/6)*height_cm*diameter_longest_cm*diameter_perp_cm) as volume, (frame_diam*frame_diam*pi()*5/4) as area from veg_volume inner join (select subplot_sample.subplot_id, year, sample_period as speriod, subplot_sample.id as subplot_sample_id from subplot_sample, (select subplot.id from subplot, (select plot.id from plot, (select site.id from site, (select region.id from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region.id) as regions  where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=regions.id order by site.id) as sites  where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=sites.id order by plot.id) as plots  where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=plots.id order by subplot.id) as subplots  where (( subplot_sample.year='16' or subplot_sample.year='17' ) and ( subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VSSV' or subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VXSV' )) and subplot_sample.subplot_id=subplots.id) as sids on (( veg_volume.species_txn='ARAR8' )) and veg_volume.subplot_sample_id=sids.subplot_sample_id order by subplot_id, year, speriod ")
vf_v597 <- fetch( res, n=-1)
dbClearResult( res)

if( nrow( vf_v597) == 0 ){

vf_v597 <- data.frame( subplot_id=NA, year=NA, speriod=NA, id=NA, dia1=NA, dia2=NA, hgt=NA, volume=NA, area=NA)
vf_v597 <- vf_v597[-1,]
}

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v597) + 1
vf_v597 <- cbind( vf_v597, t( apply( vf_v597, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v597)
names( vf_v597)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_ARAR8", "shrub_1hr_ARAR8", "shrub_10hr_ARAR8")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ARAR8 <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_ARAR8 <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_ARAR8 <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v598)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v598[i,1]
yr <- vf_v598[i,2]
sper <- vf_v598[i,3]
vf_v599 <- subset( vf_v597, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v599$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ARAR8[i] <- round( sum( vf_v599$shrub_bio_ttl_ARAR8), 0)
shrub_1hr_ARAR8[i] <- round( sum( vf_v599$shrub_1hr_ARAR8), 0)
shrub_10hr_ARAR8[i] <- round( sum( vf_v599$shrub_10hr_ARAR8), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_ARAR8[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_ARAR8[i]
  shrub_1hr_ARAR8[i] <- -shrub_1hr_ARAR8[i]
  shrub_10hr_ARAR8[i] <- -shrub_10hr_ARAR8[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v598 <- cbind( vf_v598, shrub_bio_ttl_ARAR8)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_ARAR8)
vf_v598 <- cbind( vf_v598, shrub_1hr_ARAR8)
rm( shrub_1hr_ARAR8)
vf_v598 <- cbind( vf_v598, shrub_10hr_ARAR8)
rm( shrub_10hr_ARAR8)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v598))
rm( vf_v598)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v600) + 1
vf_v600 <- cbind( vf_v600, t( apply( vf_v600, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v600)
names( vf_v600)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_ARNO4", "shrub_1hr_ARNO4", "shrub_10hr_ARNO4")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ARNO4 <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_ARNO4 <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_ARNO4 <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v601)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v601[i,1]
yr <- vf_v601[i,2]
sper <- vf_v601[i,3]
vf_v602 <- subset( vf_v600, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v602$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ARNO4[i] <- round( sum( vf_v602$shrub_bio_ttl_ARNO4), 0)
shrub_1hr_ARNO4[i] <- round( sum( vf_v602$shrub_1hr_ARNO4), 0)
shrub_10hr_ARNO4[i] <- round( sum( vf_v602$shrub_10hr_ARNO4), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_ARNO4[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_ARNO4[i]
  shrub_1hr_ARNO4[i] <- -shrub_1hr_ARNO4[i]
  shrub_10hr_ARNO4[i] <- -shrub_10hr_ARNO4[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v601 <- cbind( vf_v601, shrub_bio_ttl_ARNO4)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_ARNO4)
vf_v601 <- cbind( vf_v601, shrub_1hr_ARNO4)
rm( shrub_1hr_ARNO4)
vf_v601 <- cbind( vf_v601, shrub_10hr_ARNO4)
rm( shrub_10hr_ARNO4)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v601))
rm( vf_v601)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v603) + 1
vf_v603 <- cbind( vf_v603, t( apply( vf_v603, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v603)
names( vf_v603)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_ARTRW8", "shrub_1hr_ARTRW8", "shrub_10hr_ARTRW8")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ARTRW8 <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_ARTRW8 <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_ARTRW8 <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v604)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v604[i,1]
yr <- vf_v604[i,2]
sper <- vf_v604[i,3]
vf_v605 <- subset( vf_v603, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v605$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ARTRW8[i] <- round( sum( vf_v605$shrub_bio_ttl_ARTRW8), 0)
shrub_1hr_ARTRW8[i] <- round( sum( vf_v605$shrub_1hr_ARTRW8), 0)
shrub_10hr_ARTRW8[i] <- round( sum( vf_v605$shrub_10hr_ARTRW8), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_ARTRW8[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_ARTRW8[i]
  shrub_1hr_ARTRW8[i] <- -shrub_1hr_ARTRW8[i]
  shrub_10hr_ARTRW8[i] <- -shrub_10hr_ARTRW8[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v604 <- cbind( vf_v604, shrub_bio_ttl_ARTRW8)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_ARTRW8)
vf_v604 <- cbind( vf_v604, shrub_1hr_ARTRW8)
rm( shrub_1hr_ARTRW8)
vf_v604 <- cbind( vf_v604, shrub_10hr_ARTRW8)
rm( shrub_10hr_ARTRW8)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v604))
rm( vf_v604)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v606) + 1
vf_v606 <- cbind( vf_v606, t( apply( vf_v606, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v606)
names( vf_v606)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_ATCO", "shrub_1hr_ATCO", "shrub_10hr_ATCO")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ATCO <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_ATCO <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_ATCO <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v607)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v607[i,1]
yr <- vf_v607[i,2]
sper <- vf_v607[i,3]
vf_v608 <- subset( vf_v606, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v608$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ATCO[i] <- round( sum( vf_v608$shrub_bio_ttl_ATCO), 0)
shrub_1hr_ATCO[i] <- round( sum( vf_v608$shrub_1hr_ATCO), 0)
shrub_10hr_ATCO[i] <- round( sum( vf_v608$shrub_10hr_ATCO), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_ATCO[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_ATCO[i]
  shrub_1hr_ATCO[i] <- -shrub_1hr_ATCO[i]
  shrub_10hr_ATCO[i] <- -shrub_10hr_ATCO[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v607 <- cbind( vf_v607, shrub_bio_ttl_ATCO)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_ATCO)
vf_v607 <- cbind( vf_v607, shrub_1hr_ATCO)
rm( shrub_1hr_ATCO)
vf_v607 <- cbind( vf_v607, shrub_10hr_ATCO)
rm( shrub_10hr_ATCO)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v607))
rm( vf_v607)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v609) + 1
vf_v609 <- cbind( vf_v609, t( apply( vf_v609, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v609)
names( vf_v609)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_CHVI8", "shrub_1hr_CHVI8", "shrub_10hr_CHVI8")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_CHVI8 <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_CHVI8 <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_CHVI8 <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v610)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v610[i,1]
yr <- vf_v610[i,2]
sper <- vf_v610[i,3]
vf_v611 <- subset( vf_v609, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v611$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_CHVI8[i] <- round( sum( vf_v611$shrub_bio_ttl_CHVI8), 0)
shrub_1hr_CHVI8[i] <- round( sum( vf_v611$shrub_1hr_CHVI8), 0)
shrub_10hr_CHVI8[i] <- round( sum( vf_v611$shrub_10hr_CHVI8), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_CHVI8[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_CHVI8[i]
  shrub_1hr_CHVI8[i] <- -shrub_1hr_CHVI8[i]
  shrub_10hr_CHVI8[i] <- -shrub_10hr_CHVI8[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v610 <- cbind( vf_v610, shrub_bio_ttl_CHVI8)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_CHVI8)
vf_v610 <- cbind( vf_v610, shrub_1hr_CHVI8)
rm( shrub_1hr_CHVI8)
vf_v610 <- cbind( vf_v610, shrub_10hr_CHVI8)
rm( shrub_10hr_CHVI8)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v610))
rm( vf_v610)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v612) + 1
vf_v612 <- cbind( vf_v612, t( apply( vf_v612, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v612)
names( vf_v612)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_EPNE", "shrub_1hr_EPNE", "shrub_10hr_EPNE")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_EPNE <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_EPNE <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_EPNE <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v613)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v613[i,1]
yr <- vf_v613[i,2]
sper <- vf_v613[i,3]
vf_v614 <- subset( vf_v612, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v614$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_EPNE[i] <- round( sum( vf_v614$shrub_bio_ttl_EPNE), 0)
shrub_1hr_EPNE[i] <- round( sum( vf_v614$shrub_1hr_EPNE), 0)
shrub_10hr_EPNE[i] <- round( sum( vf_v614$shrub_10hr_EPNE), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_EPNE[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_EPNE[i]
  shrub_1hr_EPNE[i] <- -shrub_1hr_EPNE[i]
  shrub_10hr_EPNE[i] <- -shrub_10hr_EPNE[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v613 <- cbind( vf_v613, shrub_bio_ttl_EPNE)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_EPNE)
vf_v613 <- cbind( vf_v613, shrub_1hr_EPNE)
rm( shrub_1hr_EPNE)
vf_v613 <- cbind( vf_v613, shrub_10hr_EPNE)
rm( shrub_10hr_EPNE)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v613))
rm( vf_v613)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v615) + 1
vf_v615 <- cbind( vf_v615, t( apply( vf_v615, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v615)
names( vf_v615)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_EPVI", "shrub_1hr_EPVI", "shrub_10hr_EPVI")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_EPVI <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_EPVI <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_EPVI <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v616)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v616[i,1]
yr <- vf_v616[i,2]
sper <- vf_v616[i,3]
vf_v617 <- subset( vf_v615, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v617$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_EPVI[i] <- round( sum( vf_v617$shrub_bio_ttl_EPVI), 0)
shrub_1hr_EPVI[i] <- round( sum( vf_v617$shrub_1hr_EPVI), 0)
shrub_10hr_EPVI[i] <- round( sum( vf_v617$shrub_10hr_EPVI), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_EPVI[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_EPVI[i]
  shrub_1hr_EPVI[i] <- -shrub_1hr_EPVI[i]
  shrub_10hr_EPVI[i] <- -shrub_10hr_EPVI[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v616 <- cbind( vf_v616, shrub_bio_ttl_EPVI)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_EPVI)
vf_v616 <- cbind( vf_v616, shrub_1hr_EPVI)
rm( shrub_1hr_EPVI)
vf_v616 <- cbind( vf_v616, shrub_10hr_EPVI)
rm( shrub_10hr_EPVI)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v616))
rm( vf_v616)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v618) + 1
vf_v618 <- cbind( vf_v618, t( apply( vf_v618, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v618)
names( vf_v618)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_ERCI6", "shrub_1hr_ERCI6", "shrub_10hr_ERCI6")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ERCI6 <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_ERCI6 <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_ERCI6 <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v619)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v619[i,1]
yr <- vf_v619[i,2]
sper <- vf_v619[i,3]
vf_v620 <- subset( vf_v618, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v620$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ERCI6[i] <- round( sum( vf_v620$shrub_bio_ttl_ERCI6), 0)
shrub_1hr_ERCI6[i] <- round( sum( vf_v620$shrub_1hr_ERCI6), 0)
shrub_10hr_ERCI6[i] <- round( sum( vf_v620$shrub_10hr_ERCI6), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_ERCI6[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_ERCI6[i]
  shrub_1hr_ERCI6[i] <- -shrub_1hr_ERCI6[i]
  shrub_10hr_ERCI6[i] <- -shrub_10hr_ERCI6[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v619 <- cbind( vf_v619, shrub_bio_ttl_ERCI6)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_ERCI6)
vf_v619 <- cbind( vf_v619, shrub_1hr_ERCI6)
rm( shrub_1hr_ERCI6)
vf_v619 <- cbind( vf_v619, shrub_10hr_ERCI6)
rm( shrub_10hr_ERCI6)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v619))
rm( vf_v619)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v621) + 1
vf_v621 <- cbind( vf_v621, t( apply( vf_v621, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v621)
names( vf_v621)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_ERNA10", "shrub_1hr_ERNA10", "shrub_10hr_ERNA10")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ERNA10 <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_ERNA10 <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_ERNA10 <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v622)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v622[i,1]
yr <- vf_v622[i,2]
sper <- vf_v622[i,3]
vf_v623 <- subset( vf_v621, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v623$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ERNA10[i] <- round( sum( vf_v623$shrub_bio_ttl_ERNA10), 0)
shrub_1hr_ERNA10[i] <- round( sum( vf_v623$shrub_1hr_ERNA10), 0)
shrub_10hr_ERNA10[i] <- round( sum( vf_v623$shrub_10hr_ERNA10), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_ERNA10[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_ERNA10[i]
  shrub_1hr_ERNA10[i] <- -shrub_1hr_ERNA10[i]
  shrub_10hr_ERNA10[i] <- -shrub_10hr_ERNA10[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v622 <- cbind( vf_v622, shrub_bio_ttl_ERNA10)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_ERNA10)
vf_v622 <- cbind( vf_v622, shrub_1hr_ERNA10)
rm( shrub_1hr_ERNA10)
vf_v622 <- cbind( vf_v622, shrub_10hr_ERNA10)
rm( shrub_10hr_ERNA10)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v622))
rm( vf_v622)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v624) + 1
vf_v624 <- cbind( vf_v624, t( apply( vf_v624, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v624)
names( vf_v624)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_ERSP7", "shrub_1hr_ERSP7", "shrub_10hr_ERSP7")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ERSP7 <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_ERSP7 <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_ERSP7 <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v625)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v625[i,1]
yr <- vf_v625[i,2]
sper <- vf_v625[i,3]
vf_v626 <- subset( vf_v624, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v626$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_ERSP7[i] <- round( sum( vf_v626$shrub_bio_ttl_ERSP7), 0)
shrub_1hr_ERSP7[i] <- round( sum( vf_v626$shrub_1hr_ERSP7), 0)
shrub_10hr_ERSP7[i] <- round( sum( vf_v626$shrub_10hr_ERSP7), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_ERSP7[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_ERSP7[i]
  shrub_1hr_ERSP7[i] <- -shrub_1hr_ERSP7[i]
  shrub_10hr_ERSP7[i] <- -shrub_10hr_ERSP7[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v625 <- cbind( vf_v625, shrub_bio_ttl_ERSP7)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_ERSP7)
vf_v625 <- cbind( vf_v625, shrub_1hr_ERSP7)
rm( shrub_1hr_ERSP7)
vf_v625 <- cbind( vf_v625, shrub_10hr_ERSP7)
rm( shrub_10hr_ERSP7)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v625))
rm( vf_v625)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v627) + 1
vf_v627 <- cbind( vf_v627, t( apply( vf_v627, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v627)
names( vf_v627)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_GRSP", "shrub_1hr_GRSP", "shrub_10hr_GRSP")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_GRSP <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_GRSP <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_GRSP <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v628)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v628[i,1]
yr <- vf_v628[i,2]
sper <- vf_v628[i,3]
vf_v629 <- subset( vf_v627, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v629$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_GRSP[i] <- round( sum( vf_v629$shrub_bio_ttl_GRSP), 0)
shrub_1hr_GRSP[i] <- round( sum( vf_v629$shrub_1hr_GRSP), 0)
shrub_10hr_GRSP[i] <- round( sum( vf_v629$shrub_10hr_GRSP), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_GRSP[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_GRSP[i]
  shrub_1hr_GRSP[i] <- -shrub_1hr_GRSP[i]
  shrub_10hr_GRSP[i] <- -shrub_10hr_GRSP[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v628 <- cbind( vf_v628, shrub_bio_ttl_GRSP)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_GRSP)
vf_v628 <- cbind( vf_v628, shrub_1hr_GRSP)
rm( shrub_1hr_GRSP)
vf_v628 <- cbind( vf_v628, shrub_10hr_GRSP)
rm( shrub_10hr_GRSP)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v628))
rm( vf_v628)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v630) + 1
vf_v630 <- cbind( vf_v630, t( apply( vf_v630, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v630)
names( vf_v630)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_GUSA2", "shrub_1hr_GUSA2", "shrub_10hr_GUSA2")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_GUSA2 <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_GUSA2 <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_GUSA2 <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v631)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v631[i,1]
yr <- vf_v631[i,2]
sper <- vf_v631[i,3]
vf_v632 <- subset( vf_v630, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v632$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_GUSA2[i] <- round( sum( vf_v632$shrub_bio_ttl_GUSA2), 0)
shrub_1hr_GUSA2[i] <- round( sum( vf_v632$shrub_1hr_GUSA2), 0)
shrub_10hr_GUSA2[i] <- round( sum( vf_v632$shrub_10hr_GUSA2), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_GUSA2[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_GUSA2[i]
  shrub_1hr_GUSA2[i] <- -shrub_1hr_GUSA2[i]
  shrub_10hr_GUSA2[i] <- -shrub_10hr_GUSA2[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v631 <- cbind( vf_v631, shrub_bio_ttl_GUSA2)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_GUSA2)
vf_v631 <- cbind( vf_v631, shrub_1hr_GUSA2)
rm( shrub_1hr_GUSA2)
vf_v631 <- cbind( vf_v631, shrub_10hr_GUSA2)
rm( shrub_10hr_GUSA2)

rm( vf_v631)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v633) + 1
vf_v633 <- cbind( vf_v633, t( apply( vf_v633, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v633)
names( vf_v633)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_PUST", "shrub_1hr_PUST", "shrub_10hr_PUST")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_PUST <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_PUST <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_PUST <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v634)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v634[i,1]
yr <- vf_v634[i,2]
sper <- vf_v634[i,3]
vf_v635 <- subset( vf_v633, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v635$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_PUST[i] <- round( sum( vf_v635$shrub_bio_ttl_PUST), 0)
shrub_1hr_PUST[i] <- round( sum( vf_v635$shrub_1hr_PUST), 0)
shrub_10hr_PUST[i] <- round( sum( vf_v635$shrub_10hr_PUST), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_PUST[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_PUST[i]
  shrub_1hr_PUST[i] <- -shrub_1hr_PUST[i]
  shrub_10hr_PUST[i] <- -shrub_10hr_PUST[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v634 <- cbind( vf_v634, shrub_bio_ttl_PUST)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_PUST)
vf_v634 <- cbind( vf_v634, shrub_1hr_PUST)
rm( shrub_1hr_PUST)
vf_v634 <- cbind( vf_v634, shrub_10hr_PUST)
rm( shrub_10hr_PUST)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v634))
rm( vf_v634)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v636) + 1
vf_v636 <- cbind( vf_v636, t( apply( vf_v636, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v636)
names( vf_v636)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_PUTR2", "shrub_1hr_PUTR2", "shrub_10hr_PUTR2")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_PUTR2 <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_PUTR2 <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_PUTR2 <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v637)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v637[i,1]
yr <- vf_v637[i,2]
sper <- vf_v637[i,3]
vf_v638 <- subset( vf_v636, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v638$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_PUTR2[i] <- round( sum( vf_v638$shrub_bio_ttl_PUTR2), 0)
shrub_1hr_PUTR2[i] <- round( sum( vf_v638$shrub_1hr_PUTR2), 0)
shrub_10hr_PUTR2[i] <- round( sum( vf_v638$shrub_10hr_PUTR2), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_PUTR2[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_PUTR2[i]
  shrub_1hr_PUTR2[i] <- -shrub_1hr_PUTR2[i]
  shrub_10hr_PUTR2[i] <- -shrub_10hr_PUTR2[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v637 <- cbind( vf_v637, shrub_bio_ttl_PUTR2)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_PUTR2)
vf_v637 <- cbind( vf_v637, shrub_1hr_PUTR2)
rm( shrub_1hr_PUTR2)
vf_v637 <- cbind( vf_v637, shrub_10hr_PUTR2)
rm( shrub_10hr_PUTR2)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v637))
rm( vf_v637)

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v639) + 1
vf_v639 <- cbind( vf_v639, t( apply( vf_v639, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v639)
names( vf_v639)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl_TEGL", "shrub_1hr_TEGL", "shrub_10hr_TEGL")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl_TEGL <- c(0)
shrub_1hr_TEGL <- c(0)
shrub_10hr_TEGL <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v640)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v640[i,1]
yr <- vf_v640[i,2]
sper <- vf_v640[i,3]
vf_v641 <- subset( vf_v639, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v641$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl_TEGL[i] <- round( sum( vf_v641$shrub_bio_ttl_TEGL), 0)
shrub_1hr_TEGL[i] <- round( sum( vf_v641$shrub_1hr_TEGL), 0)
shrub_10hr_TEGL[i] <- round( sum( vf_v641$shrub_10hr_TEGL), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl_TEGL[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl_TEGL[i]
  shrub_1hr_TEGL[i] <- -shrub_1hr_TEGL[i]
  shrub_10hr_TEGL[i] <- -shrub_10hr_TEGL[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v640 <- cbind( vf_v640, shrub_bio_ttl_TEGL)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl_TEGL)
vf_v640 <- cbind( vf_v640, shrub_1hr_TEGL)
rm( shrub_1hr_TEGL)
vf_v640 <- cbind( vf_v640, shrub_10hr_TEGL)
rm( shrub_10hr_TEGL)
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v640))
rm( vf_v640)

calc_tcover <- function( row){
tcover <- (pi/4) * as.numeric( row[13]) / 99000
return( tcover)
}

vf_v650 <- cbind( vf_v650, apply( vf_v650, 1, calc_tcover))
names( vf_v650)[ncol( vf_v650)] <- "tcover"

calc_tlitter <- function( row){
A <- as.numeric( row[14])
tl <- as.numeric( row[9])
lmsd <- as.numeric( row[5])
lmsw <- as.numeric( row[4])
n <- as.numeric( row[8])
return( round( (tl * (lmsd / lmsw) * A * (160 / n)), 0))
}

vf_v650 <- cbind( vf_v650, apply( vf_v650, 1, calc_tlitter))
names( vf_v650)[ncol( vf_v650)] <- "tree_ltr_ld"

calc_tduff <- function( row){
A <- as.numeric( row[14])
td <- as.numeric( row[10])
dmsd <- as.numeric( row[7])
dmsw <- as.numeric( row[6])
n <- as.numeric( row[8])
return( round( (td * (dmsd / dmsw) * A * (160 / n)), 0))
}

vf_v650 <- cbind( vf_v650, apply( vf_v650, 1, calc_tduff))
names( vf_v650)[ncol( vf_v650)] <- "tree_duff_ld"

calc_tltr_depth <- function( row){
tld <- as.numeric( row[11])
n <- as.numeric( row[8])
return( round( (tld / n), 1))
}

vf_v650 <- cbind( vf_v650, apply( vf_v650, 1, calc_tltr_depth))
names( vf_v650)[ncol( vf_v650)] <- "tree_ltr_depth"

calc_duff_depth <- function( row){
tdd <- as.numeric( row[12])
n <- as.numeric( row[8])
return( round( (tdd / n), 1))
}

vf_v650 <- cbind( vf_v650, apply( vf_v650, 1, calc_duff_depth))
names( vf_v650)[ncol( vf_v650)] <- "tree_duff_depth"

calc_tltr_bulkd <- function( row){
tll <- as.numeric( row[15])
tld <- as.numeric( row[17])
return( round( (tll / (100 * tld)), 1))
}

vf_v650 <- cbind( vf_v650, apply( vf_v650, 1, calc_tltr_bulkd))
names( vf_v650)[ncol( vf_v650)] <- "tree_ltr_bulkd"

calc_tduff_bulkd <- function( row){
tdl <- as.numeric( row[16])
tdd <- as.numeric( row[18])
return( round( (tdl / (100 * tdd)), 1))
}

vf_v650 <- cbind( vf_v650, apply( vf_v650, 1, calc_tduff_bulkd))
names( vf_v650)[ncol( vf_v650)] <- "tree_duff_bulkd"
vf_v650 <- vf_v650[c( 1, 2, 3, 15, 16, 17, 18, 19, 20)]
subplot <- c( subplot, list( vf_v650))
rm( vf_v650)


calc_live_hfl <- function( row){
gd <- as.numeric( row[6])
rslt <- round( (2.667 *  gd)  )
return( rslt)
}

calc_dead_hfl <- function( row){
dd <- as.numeric( row[8])
rslt <- round(( 2.667  * dd)) 
return( rslt)
}

calc_litter_hfl <- function( row){
tlw <- as.numeric( row[9])
lw <- as.numeric( row[10])
ld <- as.numeric( row[11])
if( is.na( tlw) || (tlw == 0) ) tlw <- lw
rslt <- round( (2.667 * tlw * ld / lw) )
if( !is.na( lw) && (lw == 0) ) rslt <- 0
return( rslt)
}

calc_stand_hfl <- function( row){
sd <- as.numeric( row[12])
rslt <- round( (2.667 *  sd)  )
return( rslt)
}

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v652) + 1
vf_v652 <- cbind( vf_v652, t( apply( vf_v652, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v652)
names( vf_v652)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl", "shrub_1hr", "shrub_10hr")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl <- c(0)
shrub_1hr <- c(0)
shrub_10hr <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v653)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v653[i,1]
yr <- vf_v653[i,2]
sper <- vf_v653[i,3]
vf_v654 <- subset( vf_v652, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v654$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- round( sum( vf_v654$shrub_bio_ttl), 0)
shrub_1hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v654$shrub_1hr), 0)
shrub_10hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v654$shrub_10hr), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl[i]
  shrub_1hr[i] <- -shrub_1hr[i]
  shrub_10hr[i] <- -shrub_10hr[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v653 <- cbind( vf_v653, shrub_bio_ttl)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl)
vf_v653 <- cbind( vf_v653, shrub_1hr)
rm( shrub_1hr)
vf_v653 <- cbind( vf_v653, shrub_10hr)
rm( shrub_10hr)
res <- dbSendQuery( con, "select subplot_id, year, speriod, avg( height_cm)/100 as avg_height_m from veg_volume inner join (select subplot_sample.subplot_id, year, sample_period as speriod, subplot_sample.id as subplot_sample_id from subplot_sample, (select subplot.id from subplot, (select plot.id from plot, (select site.id from site, (select region.id from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region.id) as regions  where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=regions.id order by site.id) as sites  where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=sites.id order by plot.id) as plots  where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=plots.id order by subplot.id) as subplots  where (( subplot_sample.year='16' or subplot_sample.year='17' ) and ( subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VSSV' or subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VXSV' )) and subplot_sample.subplot_id=subplots.id) as sids on (( veg_volume.species_txn='ARAR8' )) and veg_volume.subplot_sample_id=sids.subplot_sample_id  group by subplot_id, year, speriod order by subplot_id, year, speriod ")
vf_v655 <- fetch( res, n=-1)
dbClearResult( res)

if( nrow( vf_v655) == 0 ){

vf_v655 <- data.frame( subplot_id=NA, year=NA, speriod=NA, avg_height_m=NA)
vf_v655 <- vf_v655[-1,]
}

vf_v653 <- merge( vf_v653, vf_v655, all=TRUE)
rm( vf_v655)

calc_sbd <- function( row){
sl1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
sl10 <- as.numeric( row[6])
shgt <- as.numeric( row[7])
return( round( (sl1 + (0.5 * sl10))/(10000*shgt), 4))
}

vf_v653 <- cbind( vf_v653, apply( vf_v653, 1, calc_sbd))
names( vf_v653)[ncol( vf_v653)] <- "shrub_bd_ARAR8"
vf_v653 <- vf_v653[, -4]
vf_v653 <- vf_v653[, -4]
vf_v653 <- vf_v653[, -4]
vf_v653 <- vf_v653[, -4]
res <- dbSendQuery( con, "select subplot_id, year, speriod, concat( substring( veg_volume.subplot_sample_id, 1, 2), '.', substring( veg_volume.subplot_sample_id, 4, 2), '.', species_txn) as id, diameter_longest_cm as dia1, diameter_perp_cm as dia2, height_cm as hgt, ((pi()/6)*height_cm*diameter_longest_cm*diameter_perp_cm) as volume, (frame_diam*frame_diam*pi()*5/4) as area from veg_volume inner join (select subplot_sample.subplot_id, year, sample_period as speriod, subplot_sample.id as subplot_sample_id from subplot_sample, (select subplot.id from subplot, (select plot.id from plot, (select site.id from site, (select region.id from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region.id) as regions  where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=regions.id order by site.id) as sites  where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=sites.id order by plot.id) as plots  where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=plots.id order by subplot.id) as subplots  where (( subplot_sample.year='16' or subplot_sample.year='17' ) and ( subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VSSV' or subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VXSV' )) and subplot_sample.subplot_id=subplots.id) as sids on (( veg_volume.species_txn='ARNO4' )) and veg_volume.subplot_sample_id=sids.subplot_sample_id order by subplot_id, year, speriod ")
vf_v656 <- fetch( res, n=-1)
dbClearResult( res)

if( nrow( vf_v656) == 0 ){

vf_v656 <- data.frame( subplot_id=NA, year=NA, speriod=NA, id=NA, dia1=NA, dia2=NA, hgt=NA, volume=NA, area=NA)

}

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v656) + 1
vf_v656 <- cbind( vf_v656, t( apply( vf_v656, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v656)
names( vf_v656)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl", "shrub_1hr", "shrub_10hr")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl <- c(0)
shrub_1hr <- c(0)
shrub_10hr <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v657)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v657[i,1]
yr <- vf_v657[i,2]
sper <- vf_v657[i,3]
vf_v658 <- subset( vf_v656, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v658$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- round( sum( vf_v658$shrub_bio_ttl), 0)
shrub_1hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v658$shrub_1hr), 0)
shrub_10hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v658$shrub_10hr), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl[i]
  shrub_1hr[i] <- -shrub_1hr[i]
  shrub_10hr[i] <- -shrub_10hr[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v657 <- cbind( vf_v657, shrub_bio_ttl)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl)
vf_v657 <- cbind( vf_v657, shrub_1hr)
rm( shrub_1hr)
vf_v657 <- cbind( vf_v657, shrub_10hr)
rm( shrub_10hr)
res <- dbSendQuery( con, "select subplot_id, year, speriod, avg( height_cm)/100 as avg_height_m from veg_volume inner join (select subplot_sample.subplot_id, year, sample_period as speriod, subplot_sample.id as subplot_sample_id from subplot_sample, (select subplot.id from subplot, (select plot.id from plot, (select site.id from site, (select region.id from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region.id) as regions  where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=regions.id order by site.id) as sites  where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=sites.id order by plot.id) as plots  where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=plots.id order by subplot.id) as subplots  where (( subplot_sample.year='16' or subplot_sample.year='17' ) and ( subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VSSV' or subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VXSV' )) and subplot_sample.subplot_id=subplots.id) as sids on (( veg_volume.species_txn='ARNO4' )) and veg_volume.subplot_sample_id=sids.subplot_sample_id  group by subplot_id, year, speriod order by subplot_id, year, speriod ")
vf_v659 <- fetch( res, n=-1)
dbClearResult( res)

if( nrow( vf_v659) == 0 ){

vf_v659 <- data.frame( subplot_id=NA, year=NA, speriod=NA, avg_height_m=NA)
vf_v659 <- vf_v659[-1,]
}

vf_v657 <- merge( vf_v657, vf_v659, all=TRUE)
rm( vf_v659)

calc_sbd <- function( row){
sl1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
sl10 <- as.numeric( row[6])
shgt <- as.numeric( row[7])
return( round( (sl1 + (0.5 * sl10))/(10000*shgt), 4))
}

vf_v657 <- cbind( vf_v657, apply( vf_v657, 1, calc_sbd))
names( vf_v657)[ncol( vf_v657)] <- "shrub_bd_ARNO4"
vf_v657 <- vf_v657[, -4]
vf_v657 <- vf_v657[, -4]
vf_v657 <- vf_v657[, -4]
vf_v657 <- vf_v657[, -4]

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v660) + 1
vf_v660 <- cbind( vf_v660, t( apply( vf_v660, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v660)
names( vf_v660)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl", "shrub_1hr", "shrub_10hr")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl <- c(0)
shrub_1hr <- c(0)
shrub_10hr <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v661)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v661[i,1]
yr <- vf_v661[i,2]
sper <- vf_v661[i,3]
vf_v662 <- subset( vf_v660, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v662$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- round( sum( vf_v662$shrub_bio_ttl), 0)
shrub_1hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v662$shrub_1hr), 0)
shrub_10hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v662$shrub_10hr), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl[i]
  shrub_1hr[i] <- -shrub_1hr[i]
  shrub_10hr[i] <- -shrub_10hr[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v661 <- cbind( vf_v661, shrub_bio_ttl)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl)
vf_v661 <- cbind( vf_v661, shrub_1hr)
rm( shrub_1hr)
vf_v661 <- cbind( vf_v661, shrub_10hr)
rm( shrub_10hr)

vf_v661 <- merge( vf_v661, vf_v663, all=TRUE)

calc_sbd <- function( row){
sl1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
sl10 <- as.numeric( row[6])
shgt <- as.numeric( row[7])
return( round( (sl1 + (0.5 * sl10))/(10000*shgt), 4))
}

vf_v661 <- cbind( vf_v661, apply( vf_v661, 1, calc_sbd))
names( vf_v661)[ncol( vf_v661)] <- "shrub_bd_ARTRW8"
vf_v661 <- vf_v661[, -4]
vf_v661 <- vf_v661[, -4]

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v664) + 1
vf_v664 <- cbind( vf_v664, t( apply( vf_v664, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v664)
names( vf_v664)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl", "shrub_1hr", "shrub_10hr")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl <- c(0)
shrub_1hr <- c(0)
shrub_10hr <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v665)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v665[i,1]
yr <- vf_v665[i,2]
sper <- vf_v665[i,3]
vf_v666 <- subset( vf_v664, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v666$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- round( sum( vf_v666$shrub_bio_ttl), 0)
shrub_1hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v666$shrub_1hr), 0)
shrub_10hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v666$shrub_10hr), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl[i]
  shrub_1hr[i] <- -shrub_1hr[i]
  shrub_10hr[i] <- -shrub_10hr[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}

rm( shrub_bio_ttl)
vf_v665 <- cbind( vf_v665, shrub_1hr)
rm( shrub_1hr)
vf_v665 <- cbind( vf_v665, shrub_10hr)

calc_sbd <- function( row){
sl1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
sl10 <- as.numeric( row[6])
shgt <- as.numeric( row[7])
return( round( (sl1 + (0.5 * sl10))/(10000*shgt), 4))
}

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v668) + 1
vf_v668 <- cbind( vf_v668, t( apply( vf_v668, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v668)
names( vf_v668)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl", "shrub_1hr", "shrub_10hr")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl <- c(0)
shrub_1hr <- c(0)
shrub_10hr <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v669)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v669[i,1]
yr <- vf_v669[i,2]
sper <- vf_v669[i,3]
vf_v670 <- subset( vf_v668, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v670$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- round( sum( vf_v670$shrub_bio_ttl), 0)
shrub_1hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v670$shrub_1hr), 0)
shrub_10hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v670$shrub_10hr), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl[i]
  shrub_1hr[i] <- -shrub_1hr[i]
  shrub_10hr[i] <- -shrub_10hr[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v669 <- cbind( vf_v669, shrub_bio_ttl)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl)
vf_v669 <- cbind( vf_v669, shrub_1hr)
rm( shrub_1hr)
vf_v669 <- cbind( vf_v669, shrub_10hr)
rm( shrub_10hr)
res <- dbSendQuery( con, "select subplot_id, year, speriod, avg( height_cm)/100 as avg_height_m from veg_volume inner join (select subplot_sample.subplot_id, year, sample_period as speriod, subplot_sample.id as subplot_sample_id from subplot_sample, (select subplot.id from subplot, (select plot.id from plot, (select site.id from site, (select region.id from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region.id) as regions  where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=regions.id order by site.id) as sites  where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=sites.id order by plot.id) as plots  where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=plots.id order by subplot.id) as subplots  where (( subplot_sample.year='16' or subplot_sample.year='17' ) and ( subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VSSV' or subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VXSV' )) and subplot_sample.subplot_id=subplots.id) as sids on (( veg_volume.species_txn='CHVI8' )) and veg_volume.subplot_sample_id=sids.subplot_sample_id  group by subplot_id, year, speriod order by subplot_id, year, speriod ")
vf_v671 <- fetch( res, n=-1)
dbClearResult( res)

if( nrow( vf_v671) == 0 ){

vf_v671 <- data.frame( subplot_id=NA, year=NA, speriod=NA, avg_height_m=NA)

}

rm( vf_v671)

calc_sbd <- function( row){
sl1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
sl10 <- as.numeric( row[6])
shgt <- as.numeric( row[7])
return( round( (sl1 + (0.5 * sl10))/(10000*shgt), 4))
}

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v672) + 1
vf_v672 <- cbind( vf_v672, t( apply( vf_v672, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v672)
names( vf_v672)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl", "shrub_1hr", "shrub_10hr")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl <- c(0)
shrub_1hr <- c(0)
shrub_10hr <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v673)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v673[i,1]
yr <- vf_v673[i,2]
sper <- vf_v673[i,3]
vf_v674 <- subset( vf_v672, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v674$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- round( sum( vf_v674$shrub_bio_ttl), 0)
shrub_1hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v674$shrub_1hr), 0)
shrub_10hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v674$shrub_10hr), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl[i]
  shrub_1hr[i] <- -shrub_1hr[i]
  shrub_10hr[i] <- -shrub_10hr[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v673 <- cbind( vf_v673, shrub_bio_ttl)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl)
vf_v673 <- cbind( vf_v673, shrub_1hr)
rm( shrub_1hr)
vf_v673 <- cbind( vf_v673, shrub_10hr)
rm( shrub_10hr)
res <- dbSendQuery( con, "select subplot_id, year, speriod, avg( height_cm)/100 as avg_height_m from veg_volume inner join (select subplot_sample.subplot_id, year, sample_period as speriod, subplot_sample.id as subplot_sample_id from subplot_sample, (select subplot.id from subplot, (select plot.id from plot, (select site.id from site, (select region.id from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region.id) as regions  where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=regions.id order by site.id) as sites  where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=sites.id order by plot.id) as plots  where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=plots.id order by subplot.id) as subplots  where (( subplot_sample.year='16' or subplot_sample.year='17' ) and ( subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VSSV' or subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VXSV' )) and subplot_sample.subplot_id=subplots.id) as sids on (( veg_volume.species_txn='EPNE' )) and veg_volume.subplot_sample_id=sids.subplot_sample_id  group by subplot_id, year, speriod order by subplot_id, year, speriod ")
vf_v675 <- fetch( res, n=-1)
dbClearResult( res)

if( nrow( vf_v675) == 0 ){

vf_v675 <- data.frame( subplot_id=NA, year=NA, speriod=NA, avg_height_m=NA)
vf_v675 <- vf_v675[-1,]
}

vf_v673 <- merge( vf_v673, vf_v675, all=TRUE)
rm( vf_v675)

calc_sbd <- function( row){
sl1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
sl10 <- as.numeric( row[6])
shgt <- as.numeric( row[7])
return( round( (sl1 + (0.5 * sl10))/(10000*shgt), 4))
}

vf_v673 <- cbind( vf_v673, apply( vf_v673, 1, calc_sbd))

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v676) + 1
vf_v676 <- cbind( vf_v676, t( apply( vf_v676, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v676)
names( vf_v676)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl", "shrub_1hr", "shrub_10hr")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl <- c(0)
shrub_1hr <- c(0)
shrub_10hr <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v677)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v677[i,1]
yr <- vf_v677[i,2]
sper <- vf_v677[i,3]
vf_v678 <- subset( vf_v676, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v678$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- round( sum( vf_v678$shrub_bio_ttl), 0)
shrub_1hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v678$shrub_1hr), 0)
shrub_10hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v678$shrub_10hr), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl[i]
  shrub_1hr[i] <- -shrub_1hr[i]
  shrub_10hr[i] <- -shrub_10hr[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v677 <- cbind( vf_v677, shrub_bio_ttl)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl)
vf_v677 <- cbind( vf_v677, shrub_1hr)
rm( shrub_1hr)
vf_v677 <- cbind( vf_v677, shrub_10hr)
rm( shrub_10hr)
res <- dbSendQuery( con, "select subplot_id, year, speriod, avg( height_cm)/100 as avg_height_m from veg_volume inner join (select subplot_sample.subplot_id, year, sample_period as speriod, subplot_sample.id as subplot_sample_id from subplot_sample, (select subplot.id from subplot, (select plot.id from plot, (select site.id from site, (select region.id from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region.id) as regions  where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=regions.id order by site.id) as sites  where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=sites.id order by plot.id) as plots  where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=plots.id order by subplot.id) as subplots  where (( subplot_sample.year='16' or subplot_sample.year='17' ) and ( subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VSSV' or subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VXSV' )) and subplot_sample.subplot_id=subplots.id) as sids on (( veg_volume.species_txn='EPVI' )) and veg_volume.subplot_sample_id=sids.subplot_sample_id  group by subplot_id, year, speriod order by subplot_id, year, speriod ")
vf_v679 <- fetch( res, n=-1)
dbClearResult( res)

if( nrow( vf_v679) == 0 ){

vf_v679 <- data.frame( subplot_id=NA, year=NA, speriod=NA, avg_height_m=NA)
vf_v679 <- vf_v679[-1,]
}

vf_v677 <- merge( vf_v677, vf_v679, all=TRUE)
rm( vf_v679)

calc_sbd <- function( row){
sl1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
sl10 <- as.numeric( row[6])
shgt <- as.numeric( row[7])
return( round( (sl1 + (0.5 * sl10))/(10000*shgt), 4))
}

vf_v677 <- cbind( vf_v677, apply( vf_v677, 1, calc_sbd))

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v680) + 1
vf_v680 <- cbind( vf_v680, t( apply( vf_v680, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v680)
names( vf_v680)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl", "shrub_1hr", "shrub_10hr")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl <- c(0)
shrub_1hr <- c(0)
shrub_10hr <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v681)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v681[i,1]
yr <- vf_v681[i,2]
sper <- vf_v681[i,3]
vf_v682 <- subset( vf_v680, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v682$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- round( sum( vf_v682$shrub_bio_ttl), 0)
shrub_1hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v682$shrub_1hr), 0)
shrub_10hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v682$shrub_10hr), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl[i]
  shrub_1hr[i] <- -shrub_1hr[i]
  shrub_10hr[i] <- -shrub_10hr[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v681 <- cbind( vf_v681, shrub_bio_ttl)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl)
vf_v681 <- cbind( vf_v681, shrub_1hr)
rm( shrub_1hr)
vf_v681 <- cbind( vf_v681, shrub_10hr)
rm( shrub_10hr)
res <- dbSendQuery( con, "select subplot_id, year, speriod, avg( height_cm)/100 as avg_height_m from veg_volume inner join (select subplot_sample.subplot_id, year, sample_period as speriod, subplot_sample.id as subplot_sample_id from subplot_sample, (select subplot.id from subplot, (select plot.id from plot, (select site.id from site, (select region.id from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region.id) as regions  where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=regions.id order by site.id) as sites  where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=sites.id order by plot.id) as plots  where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=plots.id order by subplot.id) as subplots  where (( subplot_sample.year='16' or subplot_sample.year='17' ) and ( subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VSSV' or subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VXSV' )) and subplot_sample.subplot_id=subplots.id) as sids on (( veg_volume.species_txn='ERCI6' )) and veg_volume.subplot_sample_id=sids.subplot_sample_id  group by subplot_id, year, speriod order by subplot_id, year, speriod ")
vf_v683 <- fetch( res, n=-1)
dbClearResult( res)

if( nrow( vf_v683) == 0 ){

vf_v683 <- data.frame( subplot_id=NA, year=NA, speriod=NA, avg_height_m=NA)
vf_v683 <- vf_v683[-1,]
}

vf_v681 <- merge( vf_v681, vf_v683, all=TRUE)
rm( vf_v683)

calc_sbd <- function( row){
sl1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
sl10 <- as.numeric( row[6])
shgt <- as.numeric( row[7])
return( round( (sl1 + (0.5 * sl10))/(10000*shgt), 4))
}

vf_v681 <- cbind( vf_v681, apply( vf_v681, 1, calc_sbd))

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v684) + 1
vf_v684 <- cbind( vf_v684, t( apply( vf_v684, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v684)
names( vf_v684)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl", "shrub_1hr", "shrub_10hr")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl <- c(0)
shrub_1hr <- c(0)
shrub_10hr <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v685)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v685[i,1]
yr <- vf_v685[i,2]
sper <- vf_v685[i,3]
vf_v686 <- subset( vf_v684, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v686$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- round( sum( vf_v686$shrub_bio_ttl), 0)
shrub_1hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v686$shrub_1hr), 0)
shrub_10hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v686$shrub_10hr), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl[i]
  shrub_1hr[i] <- -shrub_1hr[i]
  shrub_10hr[i] <- -shrub_10hr[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v685 <- cbind( vf_v685, shrub_bio_ttl)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl)
vf_v685 <- cbind( vf_v685, shrub_1hr)
rm( shrub_1hr)
vf_v685 <- cbind( vf_v685, shrub_10hr)
rm( shrub_10hr)
res <- dbSendQuery( con, "select subplot_id, year, speriod, avg( height_cm)/100 as avg_height_m from veg_volume inner join (select subplot_sample.subplot_id, year, sample_period as speriod, subplot_sample.id as subplot_sample_id from subplot_sample, (select subplot.id from subplot, (select plot.id from plot, (select site.id from site, (select region.id from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region.id) as regions  where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=regions.id order by site.id) as sites  where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=sites.id order by plot.id) as plots  where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=plots.id order by subplot.id) as subplots  where (( subplot_sample.year='16' or subplot_sample.year='17' ) and ( subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VSSV' or subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VXSV' )) and subplot_sample.subplot_id=subplots.id) as sids on (( veg_volume.species_txn='ERNA10' )) and veg_volume.subplot_sample_id=sids.subplot_sample_id  group by subplot_id, year, speriod order by subplot_id, year, speriod ")
vf_v687 <- fetch( res, n=-1)
dbClearResult( res)

if( nrow( vf_v687) == 0 ){

vf_v687 <- data.frame( subplot_id=NA, year=NA, speriod=NA, avg_height_m=NA)
vf_v687 <- vf_v687[-1,]
}

vf_v685 <- merge( vf_v685, vf_v687, all=TRUE)
rm( vf_v687)

calc_sbd <- function( row){
sl1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
sl10 <- as.numeric( row[6])
shgt <- as.numeric( row[7])
return( round( (sl1 + (0.5 * sl10))/(10000*shgt), 4))
}

vf_v685 <- cbind( vf_v685, apply( vf_v685, 1, calc_sbd))

calc_sb <- function( row){
id <- row[4]
bad_id <- 0
d1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
d2 <- as.numeric( row[6])
if( !(is.na(d1) || is.na(d2)) && (d1 < d2) ){
  t <- d1
  d1 <- d2
  d2 <- t
}
h <- as.numeric( row[7])
vol <- as.numeric( row[8])
area <- as.numeric( row[9])
sb_ttl <- 0
sb_1hr <- 0
sb_10hr <- 0
body <- 'as.numeric(p[1]) + as.numeric(p[2])*d1 + as.numeric(p[3])*d2 + as.numeric(p[4])*h + as.numeric(p[5])*vol'
p <- try( p_ttl[id,], silent=TRUE)
if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
  sb_ttl <- eval( parse( text=expr))
  if( is.na( sb_ttl) || (sb_ttl < 0) ){
    sb_ttl = 0 ;
  }
  p <- try( p_1hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_1hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_1hr) || (sb_1hr < 0) ){
      sb_1hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
  p <- try( p_10hr[id,], silent=TRUE)
  if( length(p) > 1 ){
  expr <- paste( sep='', '(', p[6], body, p[7], ')*10000/area')
    sb_10hr <- eval( parse( text=expr))
    if( is.na( sb_10hr) || (sb_10hr < 0) ){
      sb_10hr = 0 ;
    }
  }
}else{
  bad_id <- 1
}
return( c( bad_id, sb_ttl, sb_1hr, sb_10hr))
}

b <- ncol( vf_v688) + 1
vf_v688 <- cbind( vf_v688, t( apply( vf_v688, 1, calc_sb)))
e <- ncol( vf_v688)
names( vf_v688)[b:e] <- c( "bad_id", "shrub_bio_ttl", "shrub_1hr", "shrub_10hr")
bad_id <- c(0)
shrub_bio_ttl <- c(0)
shrub_1hr <- c(0)
shrub_10hr <- c(0)
n <- nrow( vf_v689)
i <- 1
while( i <= n ){
spid <- vf_v689[i,1]
yr <- vf_v689[i,2]
sper <- vf_v689[i,3]
vf_v690 <- subset( vf_v688, (subplot_id==spid) & (year==yr) & (speriod==sper))
bad_id[i] <- round( sum( vf_v690$bad_id), 0)
shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- round( sum( vf_v690$shrub_bio_ttl), 0)
shrub_1hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v690$shrub_1hr), 0)
shrub_10hr[i] <- round( sum( vf_v690$shrub_10hr), 0)
if( bad_id[i] > 0 ){
  shrub_bio_ttl[i] <- -shrub_bio_ttl[i]
  shrub_1hr[i] <- -shrub_1hr[i]
  shrub_10hr[i] <- -shrub_10hr[i]
}
i <- i + 1
}
vf_v689 <- cbind( vf_v689, shrub_bio_ttl)
rm( shrub_bio_ttl)
vf_v689 <- cbind( vf_v689, shrub_1hr)
rm( shrub_1hr)
vf_v689 <- cbind( vf_v689, shrub_10hr)
rm( shrub_10hr)
res <- dbSendQuery( con, "select subplot_id, year, speriod, avg( height_cm)/100 as avg_height_m from veg_volume inner join (select subplot_sample.subplot_id, year, sample_period as speriod, subplot_sample.id as subplot_sample_id from subplot_sample, (select subplot.id from subplot, (select plot.id from plot, (select site.id from site, (select region.id from region where (( region.code='JP' ))  order by region.id) as regions  where (( site.code='ON' or site.code='SC' or site.code='GR' )) and site.region_id=regions.id order by site.id) as sites  where (( plot.type='CP' )) and plot.site_id=sites.id order by plot.id) as plots  where (( subplot.treatment='CO' or subplot.treatment='FI' or subplot.treatment='ME' or subplot.treatment='BM' )) and subplot.plot_id=plots.id order by subplot.id) as subplots  where (( subplot_sample.year='16' or subplot_sample.year='17' ) and ( subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VSSV' or subplot_sample.sample_type_id='VXSV' )) and subplot_sample.subplot_id=subplots.id) as sids on (( veg_volume.species_txn='ERSP7' )) and veg_volume.subplot_sample_id=sids.subplot_sample_id  group by subplot_id, year, speriod order by subplot_id, year, speriod ")
vf_v691 <- fetch( res, n=-1)
dbClearResult( res)

if( nrow( vf_v691) == 0 ){

vf_v691 <- data.frame( subplot_id=NA, year=NA, speriod=NA, avg_height_m=NA)
vf_v691 <- vf_v691[-1,]
}

vf_v689 <- merge( vf_v689, vf_v691, all=TRUE)
rm( vf_v691)

calc_sbd <- function( row){
sl1 <- as.numeric( row[5])
sl10 <- as.numeric( row[6])
shgt <- as.numeric( row[7])
return( round( (sl1 + (0.5 * sl10))/(10000*shgt), 4))
}

vf_v689 <- cbind( vf_v689, apply( vf_v689, 1, calc_sbd))
